# AgentHandover Development Log

- **2026-03-19** — **Contra-inspired visual overhaul of onboarding UI.** Complete visual redesign of `OnboardingView.swift` inspired by Contra Wireframe Kit's design language. All text copy and functional logic preserved; only visual presentation changed. **Design tokens replaced**: Removed warm amber palette (bgWash, brandGradient, warmBrown, warmWhite, cardBg/cardBorder/cardShadowColor). New tokens: `darkNavy` (#18191F), `warmOrange` (#EA9134), `goldenYellow` (#FFBD12), `warmCream` (#FFF5E0), `lightGray` (#F5F5F5), `brightGreen` (#2ECC57). Constants: `contraRadius` 16pt, `contraBorder` 2pt, `thickBorder` 3pt. Typography: heroFont 36pt .black .rounded, titleFont 28pt .bold .rounded. **Screen backgrounds**: Screen 1 solid warmOrange, screens 2-7 solid white, screen 8 warmCream. No gradients anywhere. **Screen 1 (Welcome)**: Mascot inside 200pt goldenYellow circle with 3pt darkNavy border. Title 36pt .black weight in white. All text white with opacity tiers. Privacy badge as simple white text. "Get Started" as white-filled button with darkNavy text. **Screen 2 (Two Ways)**: Focus card gets goldenYellow background with 2pt darkNavy border. "Recommended" badge as darkNavy pill. Passive card gets lightGray background with 2pt darkNavy border. Step numbers in darkNavy circles. **Screen 3 (What You Get)**: Doc card with 2pt darkNavy border, 4pt orange left stripe, white background. Step numbers in warmOrange circles. **Screen 4 (Review Cycle)**: 40pt timeline nodes with 3pt darkNavy borders and 3pt connecting lines. "You Review" node in goldenYellow. Each node has a distinct color. Menu bar callout in lightGray with darkNavy border. **Screens 5-7**: Permission/VLM/extension cards with 2pt darkNavy borders. Granted states use brightGreen with 2pt green borders. All buttons custom-styled darkNavy filled (no `.borderedProminent`). **Screen 8 (Ready)**: warmCream background. Recording card with 2pt darkNavy border. Readiness chips with 2pt borders. 32pt .black title. **Navigation bar**: Contra two-button footer -- Back as outlined ghost button with 2pt border, Next/Skip as darkNavy filled buttons. `ContraButtonStyle` enum (darkFilled/whiteFilled/outlined) with `contraButton()` builder replacing old `nextButton()`. **PermissionStatusBadge**: Updated to use RoundedRectangle (contraRadius), 2pt borders, brightGreen/warmOrange, bold font. **No shadows anywhere** -- flat design with thick borders throughout. `swift build --configuration release` compiles clean. File changed: `OnboardingView.swift`.

- **2026-03-19** — **Redesigned onboarding experience and dynamic menu bar icon.** Two changes: **(1) Menu bar icon state**: Updated `menuBarIcon` computed property in `AppState.swift` from briefcase icons to binoculars-based icons reflecting actual system state: `binoculars.fill` when daemon+worker healthy (actively observing), `binoculars` when worker-only (processing but not watching), `binoculars.badge.clock` for warnings (watching with issues), `briefcase` when stopped/down (idle). Added `workerRunning && !daemonRunning` check in the `.down` case to distinguish worker-only state. **(2) Onboarding rewrite**: Completely rewrote `OnboardingView.swift` from 6 technical steps to 7 user-friendly steps: Welcome (binoculars hero, 3 value bullets, privacy badge) -> How It Works (side-by-side Focus Recording vs Passive Discovery cards with badges) -> Permissions (combined accessibility + screen recording in side-by-side cards with live status, skip option) -> AI Model Setup (same VLM logic, better framing) -> Browser Extension (marked optional with skip) -> Summary (checkmark seal with status grid) -> Ready (first recording card with title input + Start Recording button, or "just start observing" secondary). Added `writeFocusSignalFile()` to onboarding for immediate recording start. Window size updated from 520x520 to 600x620. All existing logic preserved: VLMMode/RemoteProvider enums, permission checking, Ollama pull, cloud config save, Keychain helper, extension path resolution, ServiceController integration. `swift build --configuration release` compiles clean. Files changed: `AppState.swift`, `AgentHandoverApp.swift`, `OnboardingView.swift`.
- **2026-03-18** — **Focus Q&A GUI in SwiftUI menu bar app.** Added a complete Focus Q&A window that detects worker-generated questions after focus recordings and lets the user answer them from the app. **(1) Data models**: `FocusQuestion` (Codable, Identifiable) and `FocusQuestionsFile` structs in `AppState.swift` for decoding/encoding `focus-questions.json`. **(2) AppState detection**: Added `focusQuestionsAvailable` and `focusQuestionsSlug` published properties; `readFocusQuestions()` method called from `refreshStatus()` every 5s poll — reads `focus-questions.json`, sets available=true when status=="pending", false otherwise. **(3) FocusQAView**: New view (`FocusQAView.swift`) with card-style question layout — header with workflow title (slug converted to title case), subtitle, scrollable question cards (bold question, gray italic context, pre-filled TextField with default), Submit/Skip footer. Loads questions on appear, pre-fills defaults. Submit writes answers dict with status "answered"; Skip writes status "skipped". Atomic file write (temp + rename) matching the Python-side pattern. Dismisses window after submit/skip and clears AppState flags. **(4) Window scene**: Registered `Window("Focus Q&A", id: "focus-qa")` in `AgentHandoverApp.swift` with `.defaultSize(width: 480, height: 400)` and `.windowResizability(.contentSize)`. **(5) Auto-open**: `MenuBarView.swift` gains `.onChange(of: appState.focusQuestionsAvailable)` that opens the focus-qa window when questions become available. **(6) Visual indicator**: When idle (not recording) and questions are pending, shows an orange-highlighted banner in the focus recording section: "Questions ready / slug / Tap to answer" with bolt icon, opening the Q&A window on click. **(7) Tests**: 12 new tests in `FocusQATests.swift` — single question decoding, pending/answered/skipped file decoding, answer serialization round-trip, skip serialization round-trip, atomic file write to temp dir with cleanup verification, status detection (pending vs answered vs skipped), empty questions array, Identifiable conformance. **24 total app tests pass (12 new + 12 existing), 0 failures, 0 warnings.** Files added: `app/AgentHandoverApp/Sources/AgentHandoverApp/Views/FocusQAView.swift`, `app/AgentHandoverApp/Tests/AgentHandoverAppTests/FocusQATests.swift`. Files changed: `app/AgentHandoverApp/Sources/AgentHandoverApp/Models/AppState.swift`, `app/AgentHandoverApp/Sources/AgentHandoverApp/AgentHandoverApp.swift`, `app/AgentHandoverApp/Sources/AgentHandoverApp/Views/MenuBarView.swift`.
- **2026-03-18** — **Enhanced focus session processing: behavioral synthesis + targeted Q&A.** Added three-phase post-generation enrichment to focus recordings. **(A) Behavioral synthesis with force=True**: `behavioral_synthesizer.py` `synthesize()` gains `force: bool = False` parameter — when True, bypasses the `min_observations` check (but not the budget check), enabling single-demo focus recordings to get strategy, guardrails, and selection criteria extracted. Wired into `_process_focus_sessions_v2()` after SOP generation. **(B) Focus questioner module**: new `focus_questioner.py` (~350 lines) with `FocusQuestioner` class, `FocusQuestion`/`FocusQAResult` dataclasses, and file IPC helpers. `generate_questions()` calls `LLMReasoner.reason_json()` with a prompt analyzing the procedure for 5 gap categories (credentials, strategy, decision, verification, scope) and returns 1-3 targeted questions. `merge_answers()` integrates user responses into the procedure by category: credentials→`environment.accounts`+`inputs[credential=true]`, strategy→`strategy`, decision→`branches`, verification→`expected_outcomes`, scope→`recurrence`. File IPC: `write_focus_questions()`/`write_focus_pending()` save pending state to `focus-questions.json`/`focus-pending.json`; `read_focus_questions()`/`read_focus_pending()` for worker poll; `parse_qa_result_from_file()` handles "answered"/"skipped" status; `clear_focus_qa_files()` cleanup. **(C) Worker Q&A flow**: `_process_focus_sessions_v2()` gains `behavioral_synthesizer` and `focus_questioner` parameters. New flow: (1) check for pending Q&A answers via `_check_focus_answers()`; (2) if answers found, merge and export; (3) on new session, generate SOP → run behavioral synthesis → generate questions → if questions, save pending state and pause export; (4) if no questions, export immediately. Extracted `_focus_v2_export()` helper for shared export logic (dedup, procedure write, OpenClaw/SKILL.md/Claude skill export, KB export, cache). **(D) Rust CLI finalize/skip**: `focus.rs` gains `finalize()` (reads `focus-questions.json`, presents questions interactively with defaults, writes answers back with status "answered") and `skip_questions()` (sets status "skipped" for default-value export). Added `Finalize` and `SkipQuestions` variants to `FocusAction` enum in `main.rs`. Uses atomic file writes (tmp+fsync+rename). **33 new Python tests pass (question generation, answer merging by all 5 categories, file IPC roundtrips, graceful degradation). 10 behavioral synthesizer tests pass (force parameter backward compatible). 13 focus session tests pass. 11 Rust focus tests pass. Rust CLI builds clean.** Files: `behavioral_synthesizer.py`, `focus_questioner.py` (new), `main.py`, `focus.rs`, `main.rs`, `test_focus_questioner.py` (new).
- **2026-03-17** — **Fix 6 P1 findings from pre-beta review.** (1) **Screenshot privacy leak**: `scene_annotator.py` only deleted JPEGs on successful annotation; failed annotations left unencrypted JPEGs on disk that `maintenance.rs` could not clean. Renamed config field `delete_screenshot_on_success` to `delete_screenshot_after_processing`; moved `unlink` call out of the success-only block; added `_delete_screenshot()` helper called on all VLM exit paths (success, failure, connection error). 3 new tests (deleted-on-failure, deleted-on-connection-error, kept-when-disabled), updated 1 existing test. Updated `README.md` screenshot lifecycle description. (2) **Onboarding dead-ends**: `OnboardingView.swift` had 3 state gaps: `ollama pull` success never set `appState.vlmAvailable`, cloud path unblocked on consent alone, "Start Observing" only gated on accessibility. Fixed: set `vlmAvailable = true` after successful model pull; set `vlmAvailable = true` after cloud config save with non-empty API key; removed `remoteConsentGiven` from VLM Next-button gate (now solely `vlmAvailable`); added `vlmAvailable` check to "Start Observing" disabled state. (3) **Stale service names in .pkg preinstall**: `preinstall` still referenced `com.openmimic.daemon/worker` instead of `com.agenthandover.*`. Replaced with correct names and added legacy cleanup that also unloads and removes old `com.openmimic.*` plists. (4) **Non-fatal pip failure in .pkg postinstall**: pip install failure was silently swallowed. Made it fatal with `exit 1`; added Python 3.11+ version check before venv creation; clean up broken venv on failure so re-install retries. (5) **Native messaging replay duplicates**: `native-messaging.ts` `resendBufferedMessages()` replayed last 5s of messages on reconnect, but daemon cannot deduplicate across reconnects. Replaced with `clearReconnectBuffer()` that empties the buffer without replaying. Updated `background.ts` reconnect handler. (6) **Query API logging**: `query_api.py` already binds to 127.0.0.1 (localhost-only). Added explicit log message about bind address, auth status, and how to disable via config. **47 scene_annotator tests + 33 query_api tests pass; 180 extension tests pass; Swift app builds clean.** Files: `scene_annotator.py`, `test_scene_annotator.py`, `README.md`, `OnboardingView.swift`, `resources/pkg/scripts/preinstall`, `resources/pkg/scripts/postinstall`, `extension/src/native-messaging.ts`, `extension/src/background.ts`, `main.py`.
- **2026-03-17** — **Fix 3 structural pipeline gaps: LLM classification, accumulation fragmentation, evidence flow.** Implemented Gaps 1, 2, and 3 from the pre-beta plan. All changes are additive with optional parameters. **(Gap 1) LLM Activity Classification**: `activity_classifier.py` gains `llm_reasoner` parameter on `__init__`; new `_classify_with_llm()` method calls `LLMReasoner.reason_text(think=False)` with 8-class prompt; invoked in `classify()` when heuristic confidence < 0.6 and source != "policy", producing confidence 0.75 with source="llm"; policy (Stage 3) still overrides. Wired in `main.py` after `llm_reasoner` creation. 5 new tests. **(Gap 2a) Intent Normalization**: `daily_processor.py` gains module-level `_normalize_intent()` (lowercase, strip punctuation, remove stop words, sort alphabetically); applied in `_detect_task_boundaries()` for intent comparison and `_group_to_task()` for most-common-intent counting, so "debugging code" == "code debugging". 3 new tests. **(Gap 2b) Stable Cluster Labels**: `task_segmenter.py` `TaskSegmenter` gains `cluster_label_store: Path` parameter; `_compute_centroid_hash()`, `_get_or_create_cluster_label()` with exact-hash and cosine>0.9 cache lookup, `_load_label_cache()`, `_save_label_cache()` with 30-day pruning; `segment()` Step 7 uses cache when store path provided. Wired in `main.py` with path `kb_root/observations/cluster_labels.json`. 2 new tests. **(Gap 2c) Broader Session Linking**: `session_linker.py` LLM semantic check range widened from `0.2 <= sim <= 0.5` to `0.15 <= sim <= 0.6`, catching both below-threshold-but-same and above-threshold-but-different cases. 1 new test. **(Gap 3a) SOP Generator Gets Evidence**: `sop_generator.py` `generate_from_passive_enriched()` and `_build_enriched_passive_prompt()` gain `evidence_context: dict | None` parameter; evidence section (duration, engagement, content) appended to enriched prompt. `main.py` loads prior procedure's `extracted_evidence` before SOP generation, passes it through, attaches as `tpl["_extracted_evidence"]`. **(Gap 3b) Decision Extractor Gets Evidence**: `decision_extractor.py` `extract_decisions()`, `_infer_rules()`, `_infer_condition_from_contexts()`, `_infer_condition_with_llm()` all gain `evidence: dict | None` parameter; LLM prompt includes selection signals and content patterns when evidence available. `main.py` passes procedure's `extracted_evidence` to `extract_decisions()`. **(Gap 3c) Procedures Carry Evidence Summaries**: `procedure_writer.py` new `_pre_populate_from_evidence()` sets `workflow_rhythm.avg_duration_minutes` from timing and builds `evidence_summary` string from selection signals, content, and domains. Export adapters (`openclaw_writer.py`, `claude_skill_writer.py`, `generic_writer.py`) render `evidence_summary` as "## Observed Patterns" when strategy section is absent. **2,821 worker tests pass (11 new tests, 0 regressions).** Files: `activity_classifier.py`, `daily_processor.py`, `task_segmenter.py`, `session_linker.py`, `sop_generator.py`, `decision_extractor.py`, `procedure_writer.py`, `openclaw_writer.py`, `claude_skill_writer.py`, `generic_writer.py`, `main.py`, `test_activity_classifier.py`, `test_daily_processor.py`, `test_task_segmenter.py`, `test_session_linker.py`.
- **2026-03-17** — **LLM reasoning layer: main.py wiring + final verification.** Wired `llm_reasoner` into all module constructions in `main.py`: `DecisionExtractor(llm_reasoner=)`, `CorrectionDetector(llm_reasoner=)`, `SessionLinker(llm_reasoner=)`, `TaskSegmenter(llm_reasoner=)`, `QualityJudge(llm_reasoner)` → `ProcedureCurator(quality_judge=)`. Added `LLMReasoner` + `ReasoningConfig` construction after `vlm_queue` init. Added correction-to-guardrail learning block in daily batch (after decision extraction). **2,810 worker tests + 100 integration/e2e tests = 2,910 total, all pass.** Files: `main.py`.
- **2026-03-17** — **LLM reasoning layer: Steps 5-8 — decision extraction, correction guardrails, outcome detection, SOP merge conflict resolution.** Wired the shared `LLMReasoner` (`llm_reasoning.py`) into four more pipeline modules for targeted Qwen calls. **(Step 5) Decision extraction**: `DecisionExtractor.__init__` gains optional `llm_reasoner` parameter; new `_infer_condition_with_llm()` builds a prompt with action alternatives and observation context, calls `reason_text()` for a specific observable condition; `_infer_condition_from_contexts()` now runs the heuristic first, detects generic fallback strings ("when choosing", "when action is"), and calls the LLM for refinement when available. **(Step 6) Correction guardrails**: `CorrectionDetector.__init__` gains optional `llm_reasoner`; new `analyze_correction_patterns()` groups corrections by step_id, calls `reason_json()` for groups with 3+ corrections to infer guardrail rules; new `apply_guardrails_to_procedure()` appends guardrail strings to `procedure["constraints"]["guardrails"]` and saves. **(Step 7) Outcome detection**: `OutcomeTracker.__init__` gains optional `llm_reasoner`; new `_detect_outcomes_with_llm()` formats last 3-5 event annotations and calls `reason_json()` for outcome/description/verification; `detect_outcomes()` now invokes LLM when heuristics found nothing or all outcomes have confidence < 0.6, merging LLM outcomes while deduplicating by type. **(Step 8) SOP merge conflicts**: new `_resolve_conflict_with_llm()` function asks LLM to choose A, B, or both for conflicting step pairs; `merge_sops()` gains optional `llm_reasoner` parameter — when step counts are within 1, iterates step pairs and calls LLM for textually differing actions, building a merged step list; for "both" decisions, step A gains step B as an alternative; `deduplicate_templates()` passes `llm_reasoner` through to `merge_sops()`. **14 new tests (3+3+4+4), all 205 tests across the 4 test files pass, zero regressions.** Files: `decision_extractor.py`, `correction_detector.py`, `outcome_tracker.py`, `sop_dedup.py`, `test_decision_extractor.py`, `test_correction_detector.py`, `test_outcome_tracker.py`, `test_sop_dedup.py`.
- **2026-03-17** — **LLM reasoning layer: Steps 2-4 — task labeling, cross-session identity, semantic quality judge.** Wired the shared `LLMReasoner` (`llm_reasoning.py`) into three pipeline modules for targeted Qwen calls with budget enforcement. **(Step 2) Task labeling**: `TaskSegmenter.__init__` gains optional `llm_reasoner` parameter; new `_label_cluster_with_llm()` collects unique what_doing/app/location from cluster frames, calls `reason_text()` for a 3-8 word workflow name; post-stitching loop updates `task_label` on all segments in a cluster when LLM succeeds, preserves heuristic label on failure. **(Step 3) Cross-session identity**: `SessionLinker.__init__` gains optional `llm_reasoner`; new `_semantic_check()` calls `reason_yesno()` to determine if two intents describe the same recurring workflow; `analyze_daily_summaries()` invokes it when Jaccard similarity falls in the ambiguous range (0.2-0.5) — LLM YES treats as match, NO or failure falls back to heuristic threshold. **(Step 4) Semantic quality judge**: new `quality_judge.py` with `QualityAssessment` dataclass and `QualityJudge` class; `assess()` builds a structured prompt evaluating completeness, evidence grounding, actionability, and gaps; parses JSON response; fail-open design (LLM failure/budget → default pass, abstention → passed=True with abstained=True); `ProcedureCurator.__init__` gains optional `quality_judge`; `execute_promote()` gates on quality assessment before lifecycle transition, returning gaps on failure. **14 new tests (3+5+6), all 131 tests across the 4 test files pass, zero regressions.** Files: `task_segmenter.py`, `session_linker.py`, `quality_judge.py` (new), `procedure_curator.py`, `test_task_segmenter.py`, `test_session_linker.py`, `test_quality_judge.py` (new).
- **2026-03-17** — **Fix 4 pre-existing safety/correctness issues from external AI review (3 P1, 1 P2).** All findings validated against actual code before fixing. (1) **P1 — GET /bundle writes unapproved procedures to live agent dirs**: `bundle_compiler.py` `compile()` called `adapter.write_procedure()` unconditionally, materializing draft/unapproved procedures into `~/.openclaw/` and `~/.claude/skills/`. Fixed by gating `compile_target` loop on `readiness.can_execute or readiness.can_draft` — procedures that fail readiness no longer get written to agent-visible directories. (2) **P1 — /bundle fast path returned lifecycle string instead of procedure body**: `query_api.py` `_handle_bundle()` set `"procedure"` to `bundle.readiness.lifecycle_state` (a string like `"draft"`) instead of the full procedure dict, and hardcoded `preflight` and `execution_stats` to `None`. Fixed by loading the actual procedure from KB, running preflight if verifier is available, and querying execution stats from monitor. (3) **P1 — SwiftUI MicroReviewView upgrade heuristics weaker than worker**: Swift `draft→reviewed` required only `episodes >= 5 && confidence >= 0.75`, while `ProcedureCurator` also requires `freshness >= 0.7` AND `no contradictions`. Swift also omitted the `verified→agent_ready` path. Fixed by adding freshness computation from `staleness.last_observed`, contradiction check from `evidence.contradictions`, and `verified→agent_ready` suggestion (confirmed within 7 days). (4) **P2 — procedure_verifier reads blocked_domains from wrong constraints path**: `procedure_verifier.py` read `blocked_domains` from the flat top level of `get_constraints()`, but the canonical schema stores globals under `constraints["global"]`. Fixed by checking both paths (flat top-level for legacy/test compat, `global` sub-dict for canonical schema). Also fixed pre-existing e2e test `test_full_pipeline.py` that expected `schema_version == "1.1.0"` vs current `3.0.0`. **Open question validated as non-issue**: `/ready` includes draftable non-executable procedures — intentional two-tier design with `can_execute: false` flag. **2,745 worker tests + 100 integration/e2e tests pass.** Files: `bundle_compiler.py`, `query_api.py`, `MicroReviewView.swift`, `procedure_verifier.py`, `test_full_pipeline.py`.

- **2026-03-17** — **Code review fixes for behavioral learning system (4 HIGH, 5 MEDIUM).** Fixed: (1) `evidence_extractor.py` time window construction — `end` was same as `start` when observation had full ISO timestamp; now extracts date portion and builds proper day-wide window. (2) `main.py` behavioral re-synthesis — was passing empty `[]` observations causing `synthesize()` to always bail; now reconstructs observation list from procedure evidence records. (3) `sop_dedup.py` evidence normalizer merge — was returning v3 procedure dict into SOP template registry; now guards with `schema_version`/`id` check to only use evidence merge on v3 procedures. (4) `main.py` `detect_variants` — was passing `int` cluster_id instead of `str` slug; now passes `task_label` or stringified cluster_id. (5) `evidence_extractor.py` one-shot extraction — was permanently skipping procedures after first extraction; now re-extracts when newer observations exist. (6) `evidence_extractor.py` event deduplication — was duplicating events from overlapping observation windows; now deduplicates by event_id. (7) `main.py` ContinuitySpan access — was using direct attribute access; now uses `getattr()` with fallbacks for dict-based spans. (8) `behavioral_synthesizer.py` — moved `import re` to top-level, renamed `db` variable shadowing to `br`. **2,745 tests + 77 integration tests pass.** Files: `main.py`, `evidence_extractor.py`, `sop_dedup.py`, `behavioral_synthesizer.py`.
- **2026-03-17** — **Transform AgentHandover from step recorder to behavioral learning system (7 phases).** Connected orphaned infrastructure modules into the SOP generation pipeline and added behavioral synthesis capabilities. **Phase A: Wire existing infrastructure** — expanded `task_segmenter.py` default_window_hours from 4→24; wired `variant_detector` (Needleman-Wunsch alignment, variant detection, parameter extraction) into passive SOP generation in `main.py`; enriched SOP templates with variant/evidence/continuity-span data before procedure_writer; `extract_all_pending()` for daily batch. **Phase F: Agent-aware export adapters** — updated `claude_skill_writer.py` with Strategy, Selection Criteria, Output Templates, Do NOT (guardrails), Workflow Rhythm, Browser Automation sections; updated `openclaw_writer.py` with strategy/selection/content sections, execution hints with API-alternative detection, credential references; updated `generic_writer.py` with full behavioral fields. **Phase G: Re-synthesis trigger** — added behavioral re-synthesis trigger in daily batch (re-runs when 3+ new observations); added pre-expiry evidence extraction in daily batch; added session linker feedback into procedure recurrence (daily/weekly pattern detection from session gaps). Added `variant_detector` and `evidence_normalizer` parameters to `_process_passive_discovery()`. **All 2,745 existing tests pass + 77 integration tests pass.** Files: `main.py`, `task_segmenter.py`, `procedure_schema.py`, `sop_generator.py`, `sop_dedup.py`, `db.py`, `claude_skill_writer.py`, `openclaw_writer.py`, `generic_writer.py`, `behavioral_synthesizer.py` (new), `evidence_extractor.py` (new).

- **2026-03-14** — **Phase 6: Runtime Validation and Execution Feedback — true environment checks, structured escalation, execution-driven demotion.** New modules: (1) `runtime_validator.py` (~170 lines) — `RuntimeValidator` with `validate_environment()` (pgrep -fi for required apps, optional URL reachability via HEAD request), `validate_post_execution()` (expected vs actual outcome type matching). Fail-open on non-macOS (pgrep unavailable). (2) `escalation_handler.py` (~190 lines) — `EscalationHandler` with `EscalationDecision` enum (RETRY, ABORT_NOTIFY, DEMOTE). Rules: 1st failure + retry strategy → RETRY; exhausted retries → ABORT_NOTIFY; 3+ failures in 7 days → DEMOTE (lifecycle agent_ready→stale via LifecycleManager). Deviations count toward demotion threshold. Modified: `procedure_verifier.py` — opt-in `validate_environment` param in preflight(), runtime checks added as real severity="error" PreflightChecks. `execution_monitor.py` — metadata field on ExecutionRecord, `_actions_equivalent()` replacing inline string match, escalation calls on fail/deviate with decision stored in record metadata. `main.py` — RuntimeValidator + EscalationHandler init and wiring. `query_api.py` — `/validate/{slug}` GET endpoint for on-demand runtime validation. 35 new tests (20 runtime + 15 escalation). **2,713 tests pass.** Files: `runtime_validator.py` (new), `escalation_handler.py` (new), `procedure_verifier.py`, `execution_monitor.py`, `main.py`, `query_api.py`, `test_runtime_validator.py`, `test_escalation_handler.py`, `baseline_scorecard.json`.

- **2026-03-14** — **Phase 5: Repeated-Work Meta Layer and Human Curation — unified curation queue, merge/upgrade/drift detection, 11 API endpoints.** Built a curation orchestrator that surfaces all review items to the human operator. Detection: `detect_merge_candidates()` finds procedures with fingerprint similarity [0.70, 0.95) with human-readable explanations; `detect_upgrade_candidates()` proposes lifecycle promotions (observed→draft at 3+ obs, draft→reviewed at 5+ obs, verified→agent_ready with confirmation); `detect_drift()` classifies staleness signals by severity; `build_families()` groups variant procedures; `build_curation_queue()` aggregates all sources with priority scoring (stale agent_ready=1.0, trust suggestion=0.8, merge=0.7, upgrade=0.6, drift=0.5). Execution: `execute_merge()`, `execute_promote()`, `execute_demote()`, `execute_archive()`. Dismissal: `dismiss_merge()`, `dismiss_drift()` with persistent tracking in `curation_decisions.json`. All actions auditable. No silent auto-merge (program rule enforced). API: 11 new curation endpoints (6 GET + 5 POST) in query_api.py with 501 fallback when curator not configured. - **2026-03-14** — **Phase 5: Curation Orchestrator — merge detection, upgrade promotion, drift analysis, queue building.** Created `procedure_curator.py` (~450 lines) with 7 dataclasses (`MergeCandidate`, `UpgradeCandidate`, `DriftReport`, `ProcedureFamily`, `CurationItem`, `CurationDecision`, `CurationSummary`) and `ProcedureCurator` class. - **2026-03-14** — **Add variant_detector module — Needleman-Wunsch semantic alignment and variant detection.** Created `variant_detector.py` (~427 lines) with three dataclasses (`AlignedStep`, `WorkflowVariant`, `ParameterExtraction`) and `VariantDetector` class. `semantic_align()` implements full Needleman-Wunsch dynamic programming (scoring matrix build, fill, traceback) with composite similarity: 0.5 semantic (cosine via `_cosine_similarity` from task_segmenter when embeddings provided, else Jaccard word-token similarity) + 0.3 app match (binary) + 0.2 domain overlap (via `_url_to_domain` from sop_dedup). `detect_variants()` aligns all demos against a reference (longest or explicit), classifies positions as fixed/divergent, groups demos by divergence signature into `WorkflowVariant` objects. `extract_parameters()` identifies fields (`input`, `target`, `location`) that vary across demos at aligned positions, infers types via regex (url/email/number/date/filepath/text), merges same-name parameters across positions. `normalize_workflow()` produces canonical steps with confidence scores, branches, and extracted parameters. Six compiled module-level regex constants. Helper `_self_align()` avoids code duplication for self-alignment placeholders. All edge cases handled (empty steps, empty embeddings, single demo). 9 smoke tests + 2,575 existing tests pass. File: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/variant_detector.py` (new).
- **2026-03-14** — **Add evidence_normalizer module — evidence-weighted step normalization.** Created `evidence_normalizer.py` (~370 lines) with `NormalizedStep` dataclass (step_id, canonical_action/target/app/location, confidence, observation_count, alternatives, parameters) and `EvidenceNormalizer` class. Methods: `normalize()` collapses multiple demonstrations into normalized steps using positional or alignment-based matching, selecting canonical actions via `Counter.most_common()` and tracking alternatives with observed counts; `merge_with_evidence()` replaces `sop_dedup.merge_sops()` "keep more steps" strategy with semantic matching that accumulates evidence counts on aligned step pairs, appends unmatched new steps as variants, and decays confidence for absent existing steps; `compute_step_confidence()` returns `observation_count / total_observations`; `build_variant_family()` groups procedures with fingerprint similarity in [0.60, 0.70) into variant families using connected-component discovery via BFS, selecting canonical procedure by highest episode_count. Imports `compute_fingerprint`, `fingerprint_similarity` from `sop_dedup` and `procedure_to_sop_template` from `export_adapter`. Uses TYPE_CHECKING guard for `VariantDetector`/`AlignedStep` (not yet implemented). Graceful fallback when no detector available: single demo returns confidence=1.0, multiple demos use positional alignment. All smoke tests pass. File: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/evidence_normalizer.py` (new).
- **2026-03-14** — **Phase 3: Canonical Bundle, Lifecycle, and Readiness Gate — 7-state lifecycle, bundle compiler, unified readiness.** Separated lifecycle (procedure maturity) from trust (agent authorization) as two independent axes. - **2026-03-14** — **Phase 2: Continuity Graph and Task Spans — confidence-ranked task continuity across interruptions.** Built a continuity layer that classifies segment relationships as `continue`/`resume`/`branch`/`restart`/`new_task` with explicit confidence scores and provenance. New modules: (1) `continuity_tracker.py` (~450 lines) — `ContinuityType` enum, `ContinuityEdge` (typed link with confidence, gap, embedding similarity, app overlap), `ContinuitySpan` (recoverable work unit with representative embedding, state machine, procedure candidates). `ContinuityTracker.build_graph()` processes segments chronologically, classifies against active/paused spans using a decision matrix (embedding similarity primary signal, app overlap supporting, time gap scaling), extends or creates spans. Safety: confidence < 0.50 creates new span with state="uncertain" rather than merging (program rule: false merges worse than duplicates). (2) `procedure_matcher.py` (~180 lines) — `ProcedureMatcher` matches segments/spans to known KB procedures via fingerprint similarity (apps 0.35, domains 0.35, verbs 0.30, threshold 0.50). Used calibrated 4D embedding vectors: CODING [0.9,0.1,0,0], CODING_VARIANT [0.88,0.12,0,0] (cosine~1.00), BRANCH [0.4,0.3,0.5,0.3] (cosine~0.56 for BRANCH range), YOUTUBE [0.0,0.1,0,0.9] (cosine~0.01), DESIGN [0.1,0,0.85,0.05], DESIGN_MODERATE [0.3,0.3,0.55,0.3] (cosine~0.79 for uncertain testing). All 47 tests pass. Files: `worker/tests/test_procedure_matcher.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_continuity_tracker.py` (new).

- **2026-03-14** — **Add continuity_tracker module — Phase 2 continuity graph for cross-segment linking.** Created `continuity_tracker.py` with `ContinuityType` enum (continue, resume, branch, restart, new_task), `ContinuityEdge` dataclass (from/to segment IDs, type, confidence, reasoning, gap, embedding similarity, app overlap), and `ContinuitySpan` dataclass (span_id, goal_summary, segments, edges, state, activity_type, apps_involved, representative_embedding, parent_span_id, etc.). `ContinuityTracker` class provides: `build_graph()` — processes segments chronologically, compares against active/paused/uncertain spans using a decision matrix (CONTINUE <60s+high_sim, RESUME <30min or <4h+high_sim, BRANCH moderate_sim+app_overlap, RESTART >24h+high_sim, NEW_TASK default), extends or creates spans accordingly; `classify_relationship()` — computes embedding cosine similarity (reuses `_cosine_similarity` from task_segmenter), Jaccard app overlap, and time gap to classify edges; `_compute_representative_embedding()` — averages frame embeddings; `_update_span_from_segment()` — running average embedding, union apps, running minimum confidence, duration accumulation; `_update_span_states()` — >4h paused, >24h completed, never auto-resolves uncertain; `load_spans()`/`save_spans()` — persistence via `atomic_write_json()` at `{kb_root}/observations/continuity_spans.json` with ContinuityType enum serialization/deserialization. Verified with 17 smoke tests covering all classification types, save/load roundtrip, branch parent linking, state transitions, running averages, and edge cases. All 60 existing task_segmenter tests pass. File: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/continuity_tracker.py` (new).
- **2026-03-14** — **Add procedure_matcher module — matches task segments to known procedures via fingerprint similarity.** Created `procedure_matcher.py` with `ProcedureMatcher` class that finds existing procedures matching newly observed task segments or continuity spans. Reuses `compute_fingerprint()` and `fingerprint_similarity()` from `sop_dedup.py` for structural matching (apps, URL domains, action verbs with Jaccard similarity). Match threshold defaults to 0.50 (lower than dedup's 0.70) to catch partial matches as supporting evidence for continuity detection. Methods: `match_segment()` builds a fingerprint from a `TaskSegment`'s apps, frame locations (via `_url_to_domain`), and frame `what_doing` verbs (normalized via the same verb map as `sop_dedup`); `match_span()` builds a fingerprint from a `ContinuitySpan`'s `apps_involved` and `goal_summary`; `_refresh_procedure_fingerprints()` loads all procedures from `KnowledgeBase`, converts each to SOP template via `procedure_to_sop_template()`, and caches fingerprints as `(slug, fingerprint)` tuples. Also defines `ContinuitySpan` dataclass (span_id, segment_ids, apps_involved, goal_summary, start_time, end_time) for use by continuity detection. All 2472 existing tests pass. File: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/procedure_matcher.py` (new).

- **2026-03-12** — **Fix P3-3: Swift 6 strict-concurrency warnings in MicroReviewView and DailyDigestView.** Both view models (`MicroReviewViewModel`, `DigestViewModel`) used `DispatchQueue.global().async` with `[weak self]` capture lists, which under Swift 6 strict concurrency is an error: a mutable `var` (weak reference) captured in a `@Sendable` closure crossing actor boundaries. Fixed by replacing `DispatchQueue.global/main.async` pairs with `Task.detached` + `await MainActor.run`, and moving the `[weak self]` capture to the inner `MainActor.run` closure where it doesn't cross isolation boundaries. Marked all `static` helper methods (`loadReviewItems`, `loadDigestFromDisk`, `parseDigest`, `buildMinimalDigest`) as `nonisolated` so they don't inherit `@MainActor` isolation from their enclosing class. Added `Sendable` conformance to all data types that cross actor boundaries: `ReviewCardType`, `ReviewAction`, `ReviewCardData` (MicroReviewView), `DigestData`, `DigestHighlightData`, `DigestSectionData` (DailyDigestView). Build verified clean with `-strict-concurrency=complete` (zero warnings). Files: `app/OpenMimicApp/Sources/OpenMimicApp/Views/MicroReviewView.swift`, `app/OpenMimicApp/Sources/OpenMimicApp/Views/DailyDigestView.swift`.
- **2026-03-12** — **Fix 2 P3 findings: stale result files and timer stacking.** (P3-1) In `_process_search_trigger()` and `_process_recall_trigger()`, a stale result file from a previous query could be read by the CLI before the worker writes the new result. Fixed by adding `result_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)` immediately after confirming the trigger file exists, before any processing begins. This ensures the CLI cannot read outdated data while the worker processes the new query. (P3-2) `SOPIndexManager.startPolling()` could be called multiple times without stopping the previous timer, causing stacked timers that fire redundant `loadIndex()` calls. Fixed by adding `timer?.invalidate(); timer = nil` at the top of `startPolling()` before creating the new timer. - **2026-03-11** — **Four new worker modules: TrustAdvisor, SessionLinker, DailyDigest, KBSync.** (1) `trust_advisor.py` (~200 lines): `TrustSuggestion` dataclass and `TrustAdvisor` class. Analyzes execution history from `observations/executions.json` and suggests trust-level promotions (observe->suggest->draft->execute_with_approval->autonomous). Never auto-promotes — human must call `accept_suggestion()`. Methods: `evaluate_all()`, `evaluate_procedure()`, `get_suggestions()`, `accept_suggestion()`, `dismiss_suggestion()`. Configurable `min_observations` (default 3) and `min_success_rate` (default 0.90). Deduplicates pending suggestions. Persisted at `observations/trust_suggestions.json`. (2) `session_linker.py` (~250 lines): `LinkedTask` dataclass and `SessionLinker` class. Links recurring tasks across daily summaries using Jaccard similarity (>=0.4 threshold) on normalized intent tokens (lowercase, no punctuation, stop words removed, single-char filtered). Also links by matching procedure slug. Tracks total duration, span days, status (active/completed/stale). Stale after 14 days of inactivity. Persisted at `observations/session_links.json`. (3) `daily_digest.py` (~250 lines): `DigestHighlight`, `DigestSection`, `DailyDigest` dataclasses and `DigestGenerator` class. Generates structured daily summaries with stats (active hours, tasks completed, procedures observed), highlights (new procedures P1, trust suggestions P2, patterns P2, milestones P3), and sections (tasks, applications used). Summary text is programmatic, no LLM. Save/load at `observations/digests/{date}.json`. (4) `kb_sync.py` (~280 lines): `SyncManifest`, `SyncDiff`, `SyncResult` dataclasses and `KBSync` class. Export KB as zip bundle with manifest (SHA-256 checksums, sizes, timestamps). Import with merge or replace strategy. Directory-to-directory sync with push/pull/merge modes (newest wins for conflicts). Sync state at `.sync_state.json`. Tests: `test_trust_advisor.py` (30 tests), `test_session_linker.py` (28 tests), `test_daily_digest.py` (27 tests), `test_kb_sync.py` (31 tests). **All 116 tests pass.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/trust_advisor.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/session_linker.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/daily_digest.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/kb_sync.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_trust_advisor.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_session_linker.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_daily_digest.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_kb_sync.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Team Knowledge Sharing module created.** New `team_sharing.py` (~280 lines) with `SharedProcedure` and `ImportResult` dataclasses, and `TeamSharing` class. Enables exporting and importing anonymized procedures for team sharing. Features: (1) `export_procedures()` — exports procedures from KB with optional slug and tag filtering, anonymizes each via `anonymize_procedure()`, packages as `SharedProcedure` with UUID share_id, machine alias, and timestamp. (2) `export_to_file()` — writes export envelope to JSON file using atomic write (tmp+fsync+rename), format version "1.0" with `openmimic_shared_procedures`, `exported_at`, `exported_by`, and `procedures` array. (3) `import_from_file()` — reads JSON export file, deserializes `SharedProcedure` entries, delegates to `import_procedures()`. Handles missing/invalid files gracefully. (4) `import_procedures()` — imports shared procedures into KB with conflict detection (skips existing slugs, no overwrite), sets configurable trust_level on imported procedure constraints, tags metadata with `imported=True`, `shared_by`, `share_id`, and `imported_at`. (5) `anonymize_procedure()` — deep-copies procedure and strips PII: emails replaced with `<email>`, home paths (`/Users/name/`, `/home/name/`) normalized to `~/`, IP addresses replaced with `<ip>`, auth query parameters (`token`, `session`, `key`, `auth`, `secret`, `password`, `api_key`) removed entirely, `evidence` and `staleness` sections removed. Preserves step structure, app names, generic URLs, variable definitions, tags, title, description. (6) `_strip_pii_from_value()` — recursive PII stripping for str/dict/list with passthrough for int/float/bool/None. (7) `_strip_pii_from_string()` — applies all 4 PII regex patterns. New `test_team_sharing.py` with 15 test classes and **51 tests** covering: export single (3 — by slug, share_id, nonexistent), export all (3 — all procs, empty KB, tag filter), anonymize emails (3 — step input, description, multiple), anonymize home paths (2 — macOS, Linux), anonymize auth params (3 — token, api_key, multiple), anonymize IPs (2 — step, description), evidence/staleness removal (2), step structure preservation (6 — count, actions, apps, inputs, title, no mutation of original), file export (3 — valid JSON format, exported_at, empty KB), file import (3 — round-trip, nonexistent file, invalid JSON), import conflicts (2 — existing slug, new slug), import trust level (2 — default observe, custom), import skip duplicates (1), import metadata (1 — imported flag/shared_by/share_id), round-trip (2 — preserves steps, strips evidence), nested PII stripping (3 — nested dict, nested list, mixed types), edge cases (11 — empty proc, no PII, None values, numerics, booleans, dataclass defaults, import result, non-dict file, slugs+tags combined, URL base preservation). **All 51 tests pass.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/team_sharing.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_team_sharing.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Correction Feedback Loop module created.** New `correction_detector.py` (~280 lines) with `Correction` and `CorrectionSummary` dataclasses, and `CorrectionDetector` class. Detects when a user corrects agent output and can update procedures accordingly, closing the observe-learn-execute-correct improvement flywheel. Features: (1) `detect_correction()` — analyzes event streams using three heuristics: same-field re-edit (same app+location edited within 120s with different `what_doing`), undo/revert pattern (`what_doing` contains "undo"/"revert"/"fixing"/"correcting" keywords), standalone undo detection for events without a matching pair. Parses `scene_annotation_json` (string or dict), extracts app from `window_json`, uses ISO timestamps for time-gap analysis. (2) `record_correction()` — persists a correction and saves to disk immediately. (3) `apply_corrections()` — groups accumulated corrections by step_id (or corrected_output), applies to KB procedure when same pattern appears >= min_occurrences times. Matches steps by step_id first, falls back to original_output matching against step action. Marks corrections as applied, saves updated procedure via KB. (4) `get_corrections()` — retrieves all corrections with optional procedure slug filter. (5) `get_summary()` — produces CorrectionSummary with total count, type breakdown, most-corrected steps (sorted descending), and last correction timestamp. (6) Persistence via `{kb_root}/observations/corrections.json` using KB atomic write (tmp+fsync+rename). Graceful handling of missing/corrupt/non-dict files. Five private helpers (`_parse_annotation`, `_parse_timestamp`, `_get_app`, `_get_what_doing`, `_get_location`) safely parse event JSON fields with fallback for dict/string/None/invalid inputs. New `test_correction_detector.py` with 9 test classes and **46 tests** covering: dataclass fields (3), helper functions (11 — annotation string/dict/None/invalid/non-dict, timestamp ISO/missing, app/missing, what_doing, location), record and retrieve (4 — single/multiple/filter by procedure/filter None), detect re-edit (5 — same app+location different action, same what_doing no correction, beyond 120s no correction, different app, different location), detect revert (4 — undo/revert/fixing keywords in re-edit pair, standalone undo without pair), detect edge cases (5 — empty events, no annotations, missing annotation JSON, invalid JSON, empty what_doing), correction summary (3 — empty, counts, most corrected steps), apply corrections (6 — sufficient occurrences, insufficient, original_output match, no procedure in KB, no corrections, already applied skipped), persistence (5 — round-trip, empty KB, corrupted file, non-dict file, file structure verification). **All 46 tests pass.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/correction_detector.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_correction_detector.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Agent Query API module.** Created `query_api.py` — a local HTTP server (Python `http.server`, daemon thread, 127.0.0.1 only, default port 9477) for read-only access to the KnowledgeBase. Two classes: `QueryAPIHandler` (routes GET/POST requests, JSON-only responses, Python logger instead of stderr) and `QueryAPIServer` (wraps HTTPServer in a daemon thread with start/stop/is_running lifecycle). Endpoints: `GET /health` (status+version), `GET /procedures` (summary list: id, title, confidence, last_observed), `GET /procedures/{slug}` (full procedure JSON, 404 if missing), `GET /profile`, `GET /decisions`, `GET /triggers`, `GET /constraints`, `GET /context/{name}`, `GET /daily/{date}` (404 if missing), `POST /search` (proxies to optional ActivitySearcher, 501 if not configured, 400 for invalid body). Error handling: 404 for unknown routes, 500 for internal errors. Created `test_query_api.py` with 33 tests across 10 test classes covering: server lifecycle (start/stop/double-start/double-stop/port), health endpoint (status, version), procedures (list, summary fields, by slug, not found, empty list), profile (populated, empty default), decisions, triggers, constraints, context (existing, missing), daily (existing, not found), search (no searcher 501, mock searcher, empty body 400, missing query 400, invalid JSON 400), error handling (unknown GET/POST routes, deep path), content-type headers, sequential requests (5x health, 8 mixed endpoints). All 33 tests pass. Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/query_api.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_query_api.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Execution Monitor module created.** New `execution_monitor.py` (~290 lines) with `ExecutionStatus` enum (IN_PROGRESS, COMPLETED, FAILED, DEVIATED, ABORTED), `ExecutionStep` and `ExecutionRecord` dataclasses, and `ExecutionMonitor` class. Tracks agent execution of known procedures against the KnowledgeBase. Features: (1) `start_execution()` — creates a UUID-identified execution, auto-populates expected steps from the procedure's steps in KB. (2) `record_step()` — records actual agent action, compares with expected action (case-insensitive), auto-detects deviations. Supports dynamic steps for unexpected agent actions. (3) `record_deviation()` — explicit deviation recording with detail text. (4) `complete_execution()` — moves to history, records outcomes, auto-marks DEVIATED if any deviations exist. (5) `fail_execution()` / `abort_execution()` — terminal states with error capture. (6) `get_execution()` — lookup by ID across active and historical records. (7) `get_history()` — filtered by procedure slug, with limit, newest-first ordering. (8) `get_success_rate()` — per-procedure statistics (total/completed/failed/deviated/aborted/success_rate). (9) Persistence via `{kb_root}/observations/executions.json` using atomic write (tmp+fsync+rename). Graceful handling of missing/corrupt history files. Serialization via `_record_to_dict` / `_dict_to_record` helpers. New `test_execution_monitor.py` with 10 test classes and **47 tests** covering: start execution (UUID format, active record, agent IDs, step population, unknown procedures, timestamps), record step (matching, deviation detection, case-insensitive match, dynamic steps, unknown execution), record deviation (explicit, unknown step/execution), complete execution (history move, outcomes, deviation marking, unknown raises), fail execution (error recording, history, unknown raises), abort execution (status, history, unknown raises), get execution (active, historical, unknown returns None), get history (empty, completed, slug filter, limit, newest-first), success rate (no history, all completed, mixed, all failed, deviated separate, slug filter), concurrent executions (multiple active, independent completion), persistence (save/load round-trip, file location, empty KB, corrupt file, failed execution, deviations). **All 47 tests pass.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/execution_monitor.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_execution_monitor.py` (new).

- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 9: Decision Extraction + Outcome Tracking.** Implemented two new modules for the knowledge pipeline. (1) `decision_extractor.py` (~190 lines): `DecisionRule` and `DecisionSet` dataclasses, `DecisionExtractor` class. Analyzes variation points across multiple observations of the same procedure to infer decision rules using heuristic pattern matching (no VLM required). `extract_decisions()` accepts a slug and list of observation dicts (each with `steps` and `context`); requires 2+ observations. `_find_variation_points()` compares each step position across observations, detecting action variation (different actions at same step) and input variation (different inputs with same action); empty inputs excluded. Confidence = max-action-count / total at that step, rounded to 3 decimals. `_infer_rules()` creates `DecisionRule` per unique action/input at a variation point. `_infer_condition_from_contexts()` uses binary if/else framing for 2-action cases, generic for 3+. `save_decisions()` persists to KB with upsert semantics (matches on slug+step_id, appends new). (2) `outcome_tracker.py` (~250 lines): `DetectedOutcome` dataclass, `OutcomeTracker` class. Detects what changed after task execution by analyzing event metadata and VLM annotations. Five detection heuristics: `_check_clipboard_transfer()` (ClipboardChange events + surrounding app switches, 0.7 confidence cross-app, 0.5 same-app), `_check_file_activity()` (7 known file apps + annotation keywords save/download/export), `_check_communication()` (7 comm apps + send/reply/compose/message/chat keywords, 0.75 confidence), `_check_navigation_completion()` (2+ http URLs from annotations), `_check_data_entry()` (fill/enter/type/input/form keywords). Three private helpers (`_event_kind`, `_event_app`, `_event_annotation`) safely parse JSON fields with fallback for dict/string/None/invalid inputs. (3) `test_decision_extractor.py` with 8 test classes and **36 tests**: basic cases (None/empty/single/identical observations), action variation (2-way, 3-way, majority, custom step_id, second-step-only), input variation (different inputs, conditions, empty-excluded), multiple variation points (2-step, selective), confidence calculation (even split, dominant, three-way), condition inference (if/else, generic, cross-reference), edge cases (no steps, shorter observation, default step_id, whitespace/case normalization, context passthrough), save_decisions (create, preserve rules, update existing, append different step/slug, empty list, updated_at), dataclass fields. (4) `test_outcome_tracker.py` with 11 test classes and **50 tests**: empty/single events, clipboard transfer (cross-app, same-app, none, no-surrounding-apps, multi-app), file activity (Finder/VSCode/Xcode, no-file-apps, save/download/export keywords, last-event), communication (Slack/Mail/Discord, no-keywords, non-comm-app), navigation (2/3 URLs, single-URL, non-http), data entry (fill/enter/type/form, no-keywords), multiple outcomes, events without annotations (bare, no-window, invalid-JSON), private helpers (15 tests for _event_kind/_event_app/_event_annotation with normal/empty/invalid/dict/None inputs), dataclass fields. **All 86 new tests pass, 2015 total, zero regressions.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/decision_extractor.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/outcome_tracker.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_decision_extractor.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_outcome_tracker.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 8: Branch/Exception Extraction + Constraints.** Implemented two new modules for the knowledge pipeline. (1) `branch_extractor.py` (~210 lines): `ExtractedBranch` dataclass and `BranchExtractor` class. Compares multiple demonstrations (observed runs) of the same procedure to find divergence points. `extract_branches()` accepts a slug and optional list of demo step-lists. `_align_demonstrations()` performs positional alignment with None-padding for shorter demos. `_find_divergence_points()` groups actions by normalised (lowercase, stripped) text at each step position and identifies columns with >1 distinct action. `_infer_condition()` uses heuristic priority: input value > app name > error keywords > fallback "alternative path". `_classify_branch_type()` categorises each divergence as `pre_condition` (step 0), `error_recovery` (action contains error/retry/fix/correct/undo/fail), or `data_dependent` (default). Confidence is max-path-count / total-entries, rounded to 3 decimals. `merge_branches_into_procedure()` writes extracted branches back into the KB procedure's `branches` field. (2) `constraint_manager.py` (~160 lines): `TrustLevel` enum (observe, suggest, draft, execute_with_approval, autonomous) with `from_string()` parser. `ConstraintManager` class providing: `get_constraints(slug)` with global+per-procedure merge (per-proc overrides global), `set_constraint()` for global or per-procedure keys, `get_trust_level()`/`set_trust_level()` on procedure constraints, `check_execution_allowed()` returning (bool, reason) tuple, `get_guardrails()`/`add_guardrail()` for per-procedure safety rails. All state persisted via KnowledgeBase. (3) `test_branch_extractor.py` with 10 test classes and **41 tests**: dataclass fields, empty/trivial inputs (5), identical demos with case/whitespace normalisation (4), divergence detection (3-way, multiple points, 5-demo split), alignment (padding, different lengths, column count), confidence calculation (even split, dominant path, rounding), branch classification (pre_condition, 6 error-recovery keywords, data_dependent), condition inference (input, app, error, None, fallback), merge into KB (save, overwrite, noop, clear, multiple), full pipeline (round trip, positional step_id fallback). (4) `test_constraint_manager.py` with 8 test classes and **32 tests**: TrustLevel enum values and from_string parsing (3), trust level get/set (7 including persistence, overwrite, nonexistent), check_execution_allowed for all 5 levels + nonexistent (6), global constraints (4), per-procedure constraints (3), merged constraints with override semantics (3), guardrails CRUD (6 including persistence and in-procedure storage). **All 73 new tests pass, zero regressions on existing suite (1 pre-existing failure in test_sop_schema from dirty working tree, unrelated).** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/branch_extractor.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/constraint_manager.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_branch_extractor.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_constraint_manager.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 7: Profile Builder + Pattern/Recurrence Detection.** Implemented two new modules for the knowledge pipeline. (1) `profile_builder.py` (~200 lines): `ProfileBuilder` class reads daily summaries from KB and infers user profile — tool classification (browser/editor/terminal from app name keywords), working hours (typical start/end from task timestamps, avg active hours, weekend activity), account detection (10 service patterns from URL matching with daily/weekly/occasional frequency thresholds), and communication style (primary channels from comm app usage, avg minutes/day). Persists aggregated profile to KB via `update_profile()`. (2) `pattern_detector.py` (~250 lines): `PatternDetector` class with `RecurrencePattern` and `TaskChain` dataclasses. `detect_recurrence()` classifies procedures into 4 patterns: daily (>70% of days), weekly (>60% on same weekday with min observations), weekday (workdays only, >30% ratio), event_triggered (fallback). `detect_chains()` finds sequential task pairs (A->B) with confidence >= 0.3 and minimum co-occurrence threshold. Both methods use intent-based slug fallback for unmatched tasks via `_slugify()`. `update_triggers()` and `update_chains()` persist to KB triggers file. (3) `test_profile_builder.py` with 38 tests across 7 test classes: empty state, tool inference (browser/editor/terminal classification, primary apps ordering, days_used counting, edge cases), working hours (start/end averaging, active hours, weekend detection), account detection (GitHub/Gmail/Slack, frequency tiers, multi-service, dedup per day), communication style (channel detection, avg minutes, max 3 channels), multi-day aggregation, and KB persistence. (4) `test_pattern_detector.py` with 36 tests across 11 test classes: empty/insufficient data, daily/weekly/weekday/event-triggered patterns, min observation thresholds, intent slugs, chain detection (detection, thresholds, self-loop exclusion, confidence sorting, intent slugs), pattern sorting, trigger persistence (write, preserve sibling data, updated_at), slugify helper, and dataclass fields. **All 74 new tests pass, 1950/1952 total pass (2 pre-existing failures in unrelated test_branch_extractor and test_sop_schema).** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/profile_builder.py` (new), `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/pattern_detector.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_profile_builder.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_pattern_detector.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 4: Interruption/Resumption Model for task segmenter.** Extended `task_segmenter.py` with interruption-aware post-processing. Added: (1) `TaskState` enum (ACTIVE, PAUSED, RESUMED, ABANDONED, RELATED) for segment lifecycle states. (2) `InterruptionEvent` dataclass capturing start/end time, duration, interrupting app, and classification. (3) Three new `SegmenterConfig` fields: `brief_interrupt_max_seconds` (default 60), `pause_max_minutes` (default 30), `related_interrupt_max_seconds` (default 300). (4) Two new fields on `TaskSegment`: `interruptions` (list of InterruptionEvent) and `state` (TaskState, default ACTIVE). (5) `classify_interruptions()` method on `TaskSegmenter` — a 4-phase post-processor that: Phase 1 identifies same-cluster segment pairs and classifies gaps (brief <60s absorbed silently, pause <30min merged with annotation, abandon >30min marks segment), Phase 2 builds merged segments resolving merge chains and creating InterruptionEvent annotations with interrupting app detection, Phase 3 marks abandoned segments (same-cluster pairs separated by >pause_max), Phase 4 annotates related interruptions (different-cluster segments that are short and share apps with the parent). Key design decision: intervening segments from multi-segment clusters are never absorbed — only orphan single-occurrence cluster segments can be absorbed as interruptions. New `test_interruption_model.py` with 13 test classes and **37 tests** covering: brief interrupt absorption (30s Slack check, threshold boundary, no InterruptionEvent created), pause merging (15min idle, threshold boundary, intervening app), abandon detection (long gap, different app interleaving), related interrupt linking, nested interruptions (sequential, pause-then-brief), edge timing (1s over brief, 1s over pause, zero gap), no-interruption passthrough (single segment, different clusters, empty input), multiple brief interrupts in sequence, boundary cases (interrupt before/after task), different clusters never merged (1s gap, interleaved), single-frame interruptions, data structure correctness (enum values, dataclass fields, defaults), config field defaults/overrides, and complex scenarios (mixed brief+pause, abandon+resume, three interleaved clusters, interrupting app tracking, frame preservation, time bounds). **All 97 tests pass (60 existing + 37 new), zero regressions.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/task_segmenter.py` (modified), `worker/tests/test_interruption_model.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 3: Daily Batch Processor + Activity Timeline.** New `daily_processor.py` (~300 lines) with `DailyBatchProcessor` class, `TaskBoundary` and `DailySummary` dataclasses. Features: (1) Activity stream builder — parses `scene_annotation_json` from events, supports both v1 (top-level `app`/`location`) and v2 (`visual_context.active_app`/`visual_context.location`) annotation formats, falls back to `window_json` for app name. Skips events with missing/invalid annotations or unparseable timestamps. Sorts events chronologically. (2) Task boundary detection — creates new boundaries on app change, intent (`what_doing`) change, or time gap >5 minutes. Empty app/intent values do not trigger boundaries. Intent is the most common `what_doing` across the task's events (Counter-based). `is_complete` is False when the next task uses a different app (user switched away). (3) Active hours calculation — sums intervals between consecutive events within 5 minutes of each other; larger gaps treated as idle time. (4) App usage — attributes each task's duration to its primary (first) app, sorted descending by minutes. (5) Knowledge base integration — serializes and saves via `save_daily_summary()`. Updates rolling 7-day recent context in `context/recent.json` (idempotent, deduplicates by date, trims to 7 newest entries). New `test_daily_processor.py` with 15 test classes and **73 tests** covering: helper functions (parse_iso, extract_annotation/app/what_doing/location/is_workflow, minutes_between), empty/single events, boundary detection (app/time/intent triggers, edge cases with empty values), boundary properties (duration, intent, is_complete, URLs, dedup), active hours (continuous, single event, gap exclusion, 1-hour span), app usage, annotation edge cases (missing/invalid/mixed), persistence (save, overwrite, field completeness), recent context (update, 7-day rolling, idempotent reprocess, sort order, entry fields), large batch (50 events across 3 apps), process_day return (type, task_count, procedures_observed, new_workflows_detected), v1 format compatibility, and edge cases (out-of-order, app switches, all invalid, default None fields). **All 73 tests pass, zero regressions on existing 1681 tests.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/daily_processor.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_daily_processor.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 2: Activity Search + Session Recall implemented.** New `activity_search.py` (527 lines) with `SearchResult` and `ActivityTimeline` dataclasses, and `ActivitySearcher` class. Features: (1) SQLite FTS5 full-text search over VLM annotations — indexes `what_doing`, `app`, and `location` fields extracted from `scene_annotation_json`. (2) Lazy FTS5 index creation on first search/recall call; idempotent population from existing annotations. (3) `search()` method with MATCH queries, supporting filters by date (`YYYY-MM-DD`), app (case-insensitive substring), time range (start/end ISO timestamps), and result limit. Relevance scores normalised from FTS5 `rank()` to 0-1 range. (4) `session_recall()` builds chronological timeline of user activity with active-minutes calculation (5-minute gap threshold), distinct apps-used list ordered by first appearance, and date/app/time-range filters. Defaults to today if no date specified. (5) FTS5 query injection prevention via `_escape_fts5_query()` — tokens individually double-quoted. (6) `refresh_index()` for incremental FTS updates. (7) Standalone module — manages its own read-write SQLite connection, no dependency on `WorkerDB`. (8) Context manager support. New `test_activity_search.py` with 21 test classes and **76 tests** covering: FTS5 escaping (8 tests), annotation parsing (7), ISO conversion (5), active minutes (6), lifecycle (4), index creation (3), index population (4), basic search (6), search filters (4), limit/relevance (3), special characters (5), session recall basic (3), recall filters (3), active minutes in recall (3), apps used (2), defaults (1), multiple annotations (2), dataclasses (3), refresh (2), pending exclusion (2). **All 76 tests pass, zero regressions on existing test suite.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/activity_search.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_activity_search.py` (new).
- **2026-03-11** — **Sprint 5: Privacy Zoning module implemented.** New `privacy_zones.py` (~300 lines) with `ObservationTier` enum (FULL, METADATA_ONLY, BLOCKED), `PrivacyZoneConfig` dataclass for user-supplied rules, and `PrivacyZoneChecker` class. Features: (1) Default blocked apps — 8 password managers/keychains (1Password variants, Bitwarden, LastPass, Dashlane, KeePassXC, Keychain Access). (2) Default blocked URL patterns — 14 patterns covering banking, .gov, payroll, salary, benefits, password manager sites, Google signin, login/signin pages. (3) Configurable overrides — `full_observation` patterns override defaults, `metadata_only` for reduced capture, `blocked` adds to defaults, `blocked_urls` adds URL patterns. (4) Auto-pause time windows — "HH:MM-HH:MM" format with overnight support (e.g. "22:00-06:00"), multiple windows allowed. (5) Event-level checking — extracts app name/bundle ID from `window_json`, URL from `metadata_json`, returns most restrictive tier. (6) fnmatch glob pattern matching for apps and URLs; URL matching is case-insensitive. (7) Handles both JSON string and pre-parsed dict inputs gracefully. New `test_privacy_zones.py` with 30 test classes and **101 tests** covering all scenarios — default blocked lists, custom configs, glob patterns, auto-pause (same-day, overnight, boundaries, multiple windows), tier restrictiveness, missing/invalid JSON, dict inputs. **All 101 tests pass, zero regressions.** Files: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/privacy_zones.py` (new), `worker/tests/test_privacy_zones.py` (new).

- **2026-03-08** — **Short titles, category tags, and visual polish for Workflow Inbox.** (1) Added `short_title` (3-6 word concise label) and `tags` (category tags) to VLM prompt schema in both focus and passive SOP prompts. VLM now generates these fields natively for new SOPs. (2) Added `_derive_short_title()` fallback: strips noise prefixes ("The user is..."), takes core verb phrase, caps at 6 words with natural break detection. Force-writes index at startup so SwiftUI app sees latest fields immediately. Sidebar rows show tag pills, detail view shows tags and full description below short title. - **2026-03-06** — **Bug fix: first focus frame no longer carries a pre-session diff.** In `focus_processor.py`, the first frame's diff was computed against the previous annotation from `db.get_annotation_before()`, which could be from unrelated pre-session activity (e.g. reading email). This polluted the first SOP step with irrelevant context. Fixed `_ensure_diffs()` to always use `first_frame` marker for `i == 0` (no DB predecessor lookup), and added a safety net in `_collect_timeline()` that sets `timeline[0]["diff"] = None`. Added 2 new tests: one verifying first frame diff is None in the timeline, another verifying it stays None even when pre-session data exists in DB. **21 tests pass, zero regressions.** Files changed: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/focus_processor.py`, `worker/tests/test_focus_processor.py`.
- **2026-03-06** — **Bug fix: forwardToDaemon() no longer drops messages when daemon is disconnected.** Previously, `forwardToDaemon()` in `background.ts` silently dropped messages when `!isConnected()`, permanently losing content-script events that arrived during daemon downtime. Added a `disconnectQueue` (capped at 100 messages) that buffers `{message, tabId, url}` tuples while disconnected. On reconnect, after `resendBufferedMessages()` drains the native sent buffer, a new `drainDisconnectQueue()` function re-forwards all queued messages. The queue uses splice-then-iterate so if the connection drops mid-drain, remaining items are freshly re-queued rather than lost. When the queue is full, the oldest entry is evicted (FIFO). **180 extension tests pass, zero regressions.** File changed: `extension/src/background.ts`.

Changed the button to require only Accessibility permission (the true minimum). Replaced the blocking orange warning with contextual status text: green badge when extension is connected, secondary-colored info text when not (explaining native capture works, browser events need the extension). - **2026-03-06** — **List 1 Critical Fixes Complete (8 items).** Addressed all critical bugs from external audit. **(1)** ISO vs `datetime()` timestamp comparison: 4 db.py queries used `datetime('now',?)` (space separator) but stored timestamps use ISO `T` separator — fixed to `strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%fZ','now',?)`. **(2+3)** Passive segment bookkeeping: changed `INSERT OR REPLACE` to `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` preserving `sop_generated`; passive generation now DB-driven via `get_sop_pending_clusters()` + `mark_segment_sop_generated()`. **(4+5)** Extension listener leak: store+call unsubscribe fns on reconnect; daemon seq-based dedup skips replayed messages. **(6)** postinstall `exit 1` on warnings → `exit 0`. **(7)** Swift app `llava:7b` → `qwen3.5:2b` + `qwen3.5:4b` + `all-minilm:l6-v2`. **(8)** `just build-all` now includes `build-worker` + `build-app`. **All tests pass: 1274 Python, 175 Rust daemon (1 new dedup test), 180 extension, Swift build clean.** See LISTS.md for tracking. - **2026-03-06** — **Bug fix: Transient cluster IDs overwrite sop_generated + passive generation uses in-memory state instead of DB.** Two related bugs in the passive discovery pipeline. **(Bug 2)** `save_task_segment()` used `INSERT OR REPLACE INTO task_segments` which, when a re-segmentation cycle produced the same `segment_id` with a different `cluster_id`, replaced the entire row including `sop_generated`, resetting it to 0 and causing repeated SOP generation for already-processed segments. Fix: changed to `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT(segment_id) DO UPDATE SET` listing only mutable metadata columns, explicitly excluding `sop_generated` and `created_at`. **(Bug 3)** `_process_passive_discovery()` used `segmenter.get_sop_ready_clusters(seg_result)` which relied on transient in-memory cluster IDs from the current segmentation pass. Fix: replaced with DB-driven approach — after saving segments, queries `db.get_sop_pending_clusters()` for clusters with >=2 pending segments, fetches segment event IDs from `db.get_cluster_segments()`, reconstructs timelines via new `db.get_events_by_ids()` batch method, generates SOPs, then marks each segment via `db.mark_segment_sop_generated()`. Added `_refresh_read_snapshot()` helper to WorkerDB (calls `rollback()` on read-only connection to end implicit WAL read transaction, ensuring reads see freshly committed writes from separate write connections). Applied to `get_cluster_segments()`, `get_pending_segments()` (new), and `get_sop_pending_clusters()`. Fixed date-dependent test timestamps in `test_task_segmenter.py` — replaced hardcoded `2026-03-04` dates with `datetime.now(UTC) - timedelta(hours=...)` so tests don't rot over time; fixed ISO format mismatch in `test_get_annotated_events_in_window`. **1274 tests pass, zero failures.** Files changed: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/db.py`, `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/main.py`, `worker/tests/test_task_segmenter.py`.
- **2026-03-06** — **Bug fix: Extension leaks native listeners on reconnect + Daemon has no seq-based dedup for replayed messages.** Two related bugs fixed. **(Bug 4)** `initNativeConnection()` in `background.ts` called `onNativeMessage()` and `onNativeDisconnect()` on every reconnect without storing or calling the returned unsubscribe functions, causing listener accumulation. Fix: added module-level `unsubMessage`/`unsubDisconnect` variables; each `initNativeConnection()` call now cleans up previous listeners before registering new ones. **(Bug 5)** `resendBufferedMessages()` in `native-messaging.ts` replays messages with original `seq` numbers, but the daemon processed every message without dedup. Fix: added `last_processed_seq: u64` field to `NativeMessageServer`; messages with `seq <= last_processed_seq` are ack'd but not forwarded as events. Added `test_run_deduplicates_replayed_seq` unit test. **180 extension tests pass, 12 daemon native_messaging tests pass (1 new), zero regressions.** Files changed: `extension/src/background.ts`, `crates/daemon/src/ipc/native_messaging.rs`.

- **2026-03-06** — **Fixed ISO timestamp comparison bug in SQLite windowing queries.** `datetime('now', ...)` returns `YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS` (space separator) while stored timestamps use ISO format `YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS.fffZ` (T separator). In ASCII, `T` (0x54) > space (0x20), making text comparisons over-inclusive — old ISO timestamps appeared "greater than" the cutoff. Fix: replaced all 4 occurrences of `datetime('now', ?)` in WHERE clauses with `strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%fZ', 'now', ?)` so both sides use the same ISO format. Affected methods: `get_all_episode_steps()`, `cleanup_old_episodes()`, `get_annotated_events_in_window()`, `get_workflow_annotated_events()`. Updated `test_cleanup_old_episodes` to use matching ISO format for backdating. Added regression test `test_iso_timestamp_window_excludes_old_episodes` verifying old episodes are correctly excluded by time window. **30 tests pass, zero failures.** Files changed: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/db.py`, `worker/tests/test_db.py`.
- **2026-03-05** — **SOP Deduplication — structural fingerprint matching and merging.** Prevents duplicate SOPs from accumulating when users record the same workflow multiple times. **Fingerprint:** Each SOP gets a structural fingerprint composed of normalized apps (strips PIDs, bundle IDs, arrow notation), URL domains (extracted from step locations and preconditions), and canonicalized action verbs (synonym mapping: navigate→open, type→enter, press→click, etc.). **Matching:** Weighted Jaccard similarity (apps 0.35, domains 0.35, verbs 0.30) with threshold 0.70. Desktop-only workflows (no URLs) redistribute domain weight to apps+verbs. **Merging:** When match found — slug preserved (stable identity), episode_count accumulated, steps kept from version with more steps, variables unioned by name (richer definition wins), apps/preconditions unioned, title/description updated to latest VLM output. **Registry:** Cumulative `sop-registry.json` persists all known SOPs (without heavy `_timeline` data) with pre-computed fingerprints for fast lookup. **Integration:** `deduplicate_templates()` called in all 4 pipeline entry points (`_process_events_to_sops`, `_process_focus_sessions`, `_process_focus_sessions_v2`, `_process_passive_discovery`) before writing to any adapter. **59 new tests pass covering: app normalization, domain extraction, verb canonicalization, Jaccard similarity, fingerprint similarity, matching, merging, variable merging, registry persistence, full dedup pipeline, and real-world scenarios (exact repeat, evolved workflow, Amazon vs eBay separation, variable discovery over time). 152 total tests pass (59 dedup + 42 Claude skill + 51 skill_md), zero regressions.** Files added: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/sop_dedup.py`, `worker/tests/test_sop_dedup.py`. Files changed: `worker/src/oc_apprentice_worker/main.py`.
- **2026-03-04** — **Claude Code Skill Export Adapter.** New `ClaudeSkillWriter` adapter that transforms SOP templates into native Claude Code skill files (`~/.claude/skills/<slug>/SKILL.md`). Tool derivation maps apps to Claude Code tools (browser → Bash, terminal/IDE → Bash, filesystem → Read/Write, unknown → broad access). Variable substitution converts `{{name}}` → `$N`.
