Files changed: `crates/daemon/src/lib.rs` (added `pub mod ipc`).
- **2026-02-16** — Task 30: Phase 1 Integration Test. Created end-to-end integration test suite at `tests/integration/test_phase1.py` validating the full Phase 1 pipeline: browser events -> daemon SQLite storage -> worker reads -> episode building -> negative demo pruning -> clipboard linking. Uses a real SQLite database initialized with the daemon's v001_initial.sql schema, inserts events that simulate what the daemon would write from browser messages, then processes them through the Python worker's components. 7 test classes with 13 tests total: (1) `TestFullE2EPipeline` — simulates a realistic 8-event browser session (GitHub PR review + Slack copy-paste workflow), verifying WorkerDB reads events correctly from SQLite, EpisodeBuilder creates 2 threads (GitHub and Slack), ClipboardLinker finds the copy-paste link, and NegativeDemoPruner finds no negatives in the happy path. (2) `TestNegativeDemoDetection` — 2 tests: undo workflow (5 typing events + Ctrl+Z + 3 post-undo events, verifying undo and preceding events are marked negative while post-undo events stay positive) and cancel click workflow (dialog interaction + Cancel click, verifying cancel and preceding events marked negative). (3) `TestEpisodeSegmentation` — 2 tests: 45-minute session producing 3+ segments with correct prev_segment_id chain, and 210-event hard cap split producing 200+10 segments. (4) `TestSecureFieldHandling` — verifies SecureFieldFocus events are stored with is_secure flag, no ClickIntent events appear during secure period, and events before/after secure field are present. (5) `TestMultipleClipboardLinks` — 2 tests: cross-app copy-paste (Terminal copy A + Safari copy B -> VSCode paste A + Slack paste B, both links found with correct hash pairing) and most-recent-copy selection when same content copied twice. (6) `TestCombinedPipeline` — runs all pipeline components (episode builder, negative demo pruner, clipboard linker) on a single event stream with normal work, an undo, and a copy-paste to verify they compose without interference. (7) `TestWorkerDBEdgeCases` — 4 tests: event-by-id round-trip with cursor coordinates and nested JSON, nonexistent event returns None, processed events excluded from unprocessed query, and timestamp ordering independent of insertion order. All 13 integration tests pass; all 41 existing worker unit tests pass with zero regressions. Files added: `tests/__init__.py`, `tests/integration/__init__.py`, `tests/integration/test_phase1.py`.
- **2026-02-16** — Tasks 21+22: Viewport-Bounded DOM Snapshot Capture + Shadow DOM Piercing. Implemented the core DOM snapshot capture module for the Chrome extension. (1) `extension/src/dom-capture.ts` — Full production module with 7 exported functions: `captureViewportDOM()` (main entry point, walks document.body children and returns `DomNode[]` tree), `walkDOM()` (recursive DOM tree walker with Shadow DOM piercing, viewport filtering, depth limiting at MAX_TREE_DEPTH=30, and table/text truncation), `isInViewport()` (viewport intersection check using `getBoundingClientRect()` with MIN_ELEMENT_SIZE=1 pixel filter), `extractNodeInfo()` (semantic anchor extraction: ARIA role, aria-label, aria-labelledby resolution, data-testid/data-test-id/data-cy, bounding box with rounded values, interactive element state for inputs/selects/buttons/textareas, aria-checked/aria-selected/aria-disabled for custom widgets, input type/placeholder/value capture, password field value suppression, meaningful CSS class names as fallback name), `stripCssRot()` (filters out auto-generated CSS class names matching 4 patterns: Emotion `/^css-[a-z0-9]+$/`, styled-components `/^sc-[a-zA-Z0-9]+$/`, CSS Modules `/^[a-zA-Z]+_[a-zA-Z]+__[a-z0-9]+$/`, generic hash with digit requirement `/^[a-z]{1,4}-(?=[a-z0-9]*[0-9])[a-z0-9]{4,12}$/`), `isCssRot()` (single class check), `truncateText()` (MAX_TEXT_LENGTH=500 with word-boundary-aware truncation and ellipsis marker), `truncateTable()` (MAX_TABLE_ROWS=50, preserves thead/tfoot, includes only visible tbody rows, adds `#truncated` marker node with count). Shadow DOM piercing: when an element has an open `shadowRoot`, recursively walks its children and marks resulting `DomNode`s with `isShadowRoot: true`. Filters hidden elements (hidden attribute, display:none, visibility:hidden), script/style/svg/canvas/iframe/template tags, and zero-size elements. Captures direct text content for inline elements (a, button, span, p, h1-h6, etc.) without duplicating descendant text. (2) `extension/src/types.ts` — Added `isShadowRoot?: boolean` field to `DomNode` interface. (3) `extension/src/content.ts` — Wired `captureViewportDOM` import; `request_snapshot` handler now captures viewport DOM, logs node count, and sends `dom_snapshot` message to background. (4) `extension/tests/dom-capture.test.ts` — 69 tests across 8 describe blocks: CSS rot stripping (9 tests: Emotion, styled-components, CSS Modules, generic hash removal; Tailwind, BEM, semantic preservation; empty input; all-rot input), isCssRot single-class check (5 tests), text truncation (7 tests: short passthrough, exact length, long truncation with ellipsis, word boundary breaking, hard limit when no boundary, custom maxChars, empty string), viewport intersection (12 tests: fully inside, 4 partially visible edges, 4 fully outside directions, zero-width, zero-height, full-span), semantic info extraction (14 tests: tag, role, aria-label, data-testid, data-test-id, data-cy, bbox rounding, disabled input, checked checkbox with type tag, placeholder as name, password suppression, select option, aria-checked/aria-disabled custom widgets, CSS rot class stripping from name, aria-labelledby resolution), table truncation (3 tests: thead preservation, row truncation with marker, no marker when all fit), walkDOM (6 tests: text node null, script null, style null, hidden null, off-screen null, simple visible capture, nested capture, MAX_TREE_DEPTH enforcement, table capture), captureViewportDOM integration (4 tests: empty body, visible vs off-screen filtering, ARIA capture, interactive state, multiple children), constants verification (3 tests). (5) `extension/tests/shadow-dom.test.ts` — 12 tests across 6 describe blocks: single-level Shadow DOM (3 tests: open shadow root traversal, isShadowRoot marking, multiple shadow children), nested multi-level (2 tests: 2-level and 3-level piercing with chain navigation), mixed light+shadow DOM (1 test: both children included, correct isShadowRoot marking), semantic extraction from shadow elements (3 tests: ARIA attributes, interactive checkbox state, bbox), captureViewportDOM with Shadow DOM (2 tests: full page integration, multiple shadow hosts), viewport filtering within shadow trees (1 test: off-screen shadow elements filtered). All 133 tests pass (69 dom-capture + 12 shadow-dom + 52 pre-existing). Webpack build compiles successfully (content.js 9.6 KB). Files added: `extension/src/dom-capture.ts`, `extension/tests/dom-capture.test.ts`, `extension/tests/shadow-dom.test.ts`. Files changed: `extension/src/types.ts` (added `isShadowRoot` field to `DomNode`), `extension/src/content.ts` (added `captureViewportDOM` import and snapshot handler), `extension/package.json` (added `test` and `test:watch` scripts).
